msg:i have stayed in many hotels over many years in East Asia. The Tianhan Jingyi Park Hotel and Resort is by far the best hotel i have ever stayed at. It is truly a 'resort' as the grounds are wonderful to walk around in. The staff are superb. Very polite and helpful. I will be visiting Hanzhong again on business, hopefully next year and will definitely stay at this hotel resort again. I cannot find any faults with it.

msg:It is the best star hotel in Hanzhong, but the overall price/performance ratio is not high.
The overall decoration style is very modern and luxurious, the surrounding wetland park scenery is beautiful, and the night view is also beautiful.

The room facilities are good and have the conditions required for a 4-star hotel. The breakfast is quite rich and delicious, but not as good as a chain four or five-star hotel. The service level also needs to be improved.

There is a Pacific Cafe in the hotel, as well as a book bar, afternoon tea, etc.

It is very suitable for a family of all ages to have a vacation here.
